expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    \n    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "access"})\n    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode,     payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.JWT_SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.JWT_ALGORITHM])\n        return payload\n    except JWTError:\n        return None\n\n\n# Vault encryption (zero-knowledge)\nclass VaultEncryption:\n    """Zero-knowledge vault encryption."""\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def derive_key(master_password: str, salt: bytes) -> bytes:\n        """Derive encryption key from master password."""\n        kdf = PBKDF2(\n            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),\n            length=32,\n            salt=salt,\n            iterations=100000,\n            backend=default_backend()\n        )\n        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(kdf.derive(master_password.encode()))\n    \n    @staticmethod\n    def encrypt_vault(data: str, master_password: str,       """Decrypt vault data with master password."""\n        key = VaultEncryption.derive_key(master_password, salt)\n        f = Fernet(key)\n        encrypted_bytes =  """Generate random salt."""\n        return secrets.token_bytes(32)\n\n\n# Password encryption (AES-256)\nclass PasswordEncryption:\n    """AES-256 password encryption."""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.key = settings.VAULT_ENCRYPTION_KEY.encode()[:32]\n        self.fernet = Fernet(base64.urlsafe_b64encode(self.key))\n    \n    def encrypt(self, password: str) -> str:\n        """Encrypt password."""\n        encrypted = self.fernet.encrypt(password.encode())\n        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(encrypted).decode()\n    \n    def decrypt(self, encrypted_password: str) -> str:\n        """Decrypt password."""\n        encrypted_bytes = base64.urlsafe_b64decode(encrypted_password.encode())\n        decrypted = self.fernet.decrypt(encrypted_bytes)\n        return decrypted.decode()\n\n\npassword_encryption = PasswordEncryption()\n\n\n# Password generation\ndef generate_password(\n    length: int = 16,\n    use_uppercase: bool = True,\n    use_lowercase: bool = True,\n    use_digits: bool = True,\n    use_symbols: bool = True,\n    exclude_ambiguous: bool = True\n) -> str:\n    """Generate secure random password."""\n    chars = ""\n    \n    if use_lowercase:\n        chars += string.ascii_lowercase\n    if use_uppercase:\n        chars += string.ascii_uppercase\n    if use_digits:\n        chars += string.digits\n    if use_symbols:\n        chars += "!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?"\n    \n    if exclude_ambiguous:\n        # Remove ambiguous characters\n        ambiguous = "il1Lo0O"\n        chars = "".join(c for c in chars if c not in ambiguous)\n    \n    if not chars:\n        raise ValueError("At least one character type must be selected")\n    \n    # Ensure at least one character from each selected type\n    password = []\n    if use_lowercase:\n        password.append(secrets.choice(string.ascii_lowercase))\n    if use_uppercase:\n        password.append(secrets.choice(string.ascii_uppercase))\n    if use_digits:\n        password.append(secrets.choice(string.digits))\n    if use_symbols:\n        password.append(secrets.choice("!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?"))\n    \n    # Fill remaining length\n    for _ in range(length - len(password)):\n        password.append(secrets.choice(chars))\n    \n    # Shuffle\n    secrets.SystemRandom().shuffle(password)\n    \n    return "".join(password)\n\n\n# Password strength analysis\ndef analyze_password_strength(password: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    """Analyze password strength."""\n    score = 0\n    feedback = []\n    \n    # Length check\n    length = len(password)\n    if length < 8:\n        feedback.append("Password is too short (minimum 8 characters)")\n    elif length < 12:\n        score += 1\n        feedback.append("Consider using a longer password (12+ characters)")\n    elif length < 16:\n        score += 2\n    else:\n        score += 3\n    \n    # Character variety\n    has_lower = any(c.islower() for c in password)\n    has_upper = any(c.isupper() for c in password)\n    has_digit = any(c.isdigit() for c in password)\n    has_symbol = any(c in "!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?" for c in password)\n    \n    variety = sum([has_lower, has_upper, has_digit, has_symbol])\n    score += variety\n    \n    if not has_lower:\n        feedback.append("Add lowercase letters")\n    if not has_upper:\n        feedback.append("Add uppercase letters")\n    if not has_digit:\n        feedback.append("Add numbers")\n    if not has_symbol:\n        feedback.append("Add symbols")\n    \n    # Common patterns\n    common_passwords = ["password", "123456", "qwerty", "admin", "letmein"]\n    if password.lower() in common_passwords:\n        score = 0\n        feedback.append("This is a commonly used password")\n    \n    # Sequential characters\n    if any(password[i:i+3].isdigit() and int(password[i:i+3]) in range(100, 1000) \n           for i in range(len(password) - 2)):\n        score -= 1\n        feedback.append("Avoid sequential numbers")\n    \n    # Determine strength level\n    if score <= 2:\n        strength = "weak"\n        color = "red"\n    elif score <= 4:\n        strength = "fair"\n        color = "orange"\n    elif score <= 6:\n        strength = "good"\n        color = "yellow"\n    else:\n        strength = "strong"\n        color = "green"\n    \n    return {\n        "score": max(0, min(score, 10)),\n        "strength": strength,\n        "color": color,\n        "feedback": feedback if feedback else ["Password looks good!"]\n    }\n\n\n# 2FA\ndef generate_totp_secret() -> str:\n    """Generate TOTP secret for 2FA."""\n    return pyotp.random_base32()\n\n\ndef verify_totp(secret: str, token: str) -> bool:\n    """Verify TOTP token."""\n    totp = pyotp.TOTP(secret)\n    return totp.verify(token, valid_window=1)\n\n\ndef get_totp_uri(secret: str, email: str) -> str:\n    """Get TOTP URI for QR code."""\n    return key."""\n    return f"psp_{secrets.token_urlsafe(32)}"\n\n\n# Hash API key for storage\ndef hash_api_key(api_key: str) -> str:\n    """Hash API key for secure storage."""\n    return hashlib.sha256(api_key.encode()).hexdigest()\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="passport/backend/app/api/deps.py">\n"""\nAPI dependencies for authentication and authorization.\n"""\nfrom typing import Optional, Generator\nfrom fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status, Header\nfrom fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials\nfrom sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession\nfrom sqlalchemy import select\nfrom ..db.database import get_db\nfrom ..models.user import User, APIKey\nfrom ..core.security import decode_token, hash_api_key\nimport json\n\nsecurity = HTTPBearer()\n\n\nasync def get_current_user(\n    credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current authenticated user from JWT token."""\n    token = credentials.credentials\n    \n    # Decode token\n    payload = decode_token(token)\n    if not payload:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid authentication credentials",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n    \n    # Check token type\n    if payload.get("type") != "access":\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid token type",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n    \n    # Get user\n    user_id = payload.get("sub")\n    if not user_id:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid token payload",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n    \n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == int(user_id)))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="User not found",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n    \n    if not user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="User account is inactive"\n        )\n    \n    return user\n\n\nasync def get_current_active_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current active user."""\n    if not current_user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="User account is inactive"\n        )\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def get_current_verified_user(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n) -> User:\n    """Get current verified user."""\n    if not current_user.is_verified:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="Email not verified"\n        )\n    return current_user\n\n\nasync def get_user_from_api_key(\n    x_api_key: Optional[str] = Header(None),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Optional[User]:\n    """Get user from API key."""\n    if not x_api_key:\n        return None\n    \n    # Hash the API key\n    key_hash = hash_api_key(x_api_key)\n    \n    # Find API key\n    result = await db.execute(\n        select(APIKey).where(\n            APIKey.key_hash == key_hash,\n            APIKey.is_active == True\n        )\n    )\n    api_key = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not api_key:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid API key"\n        )\n    \n    # Update last used\n    api_key.last_used_at = func.now()\n    api_key.usage_count += 1\n    await db.commit()\n    \n    # Get user\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == api_key.user_id))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not user or not user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid API key"\n        )\n    \n    return user\n\n\nasync def get_current_user_or_api_key(\n    user_from_token: Optional[User] = Depends(get_current_user),\n    user_from_api_key: Optional[User] = Depends(get_user_from_api_key)\n) -> User:\n    """Get user from either JWT token or API key."""\n    user = user_from_token or user_from_api_key\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Authentication required"\n        )\n    return user\n\n\ndef require_premium(current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)) -> User:\n    """Require premium subscription."""\n    from ..models.user import UserRole\n    \n    if current_user.role not in [UserRole.PREMIUM, UserRole.FAMILY, UserRole.BUSINESS, UserRole.ADMIN]:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="Premium subscription required"\n        )\n    return current_user\n\n\ndef require_admin(current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)) -> User:\n    """Require admin role."""\n    from ..models.user import UserRole\n    \n    if current_user.role != UserRole.ADMIN:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="Admin access required"\n        )\n    return current_user\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Now I\'ll create the main API endpoints. Let me build the authentication endpoints first:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="passport/backend/app/api/v1/auth.py">\n"""\nAuthentication endpoints.\n"""\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Any\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status, Request\nfrom sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession\nfrom sqlalchemy import select\nfrom ...db.database import get_db\nfrom ...models.user import User, Session as UserSession\nfrom ...schemas.user import (\n    UserRegister, \n    UserLogin, \n    Token, \n    UserResponse,\n    TOTPSetup,\n    TOTPVerify\n)\nfrom ...core.security import (\n    verify_password,\n    get_password_hash,\n    create_access_token,\n    create_refresh_token,\n    decode_token,\n    VaultEncryption,\n    generate_totp_secret,\n    verify_totp,\n    get_totp_uri\n)\nfrom ...core.config import settings\nimport secrets\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n\n@router.post("/register", response_model=UserResponse, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\nasync def register(\n    user_data: UserRegister,\n    request: Request,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Register a new user."""\n    \n    # Check if user exists\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == user_data.email))\n    if result.scalar_one_or_none():\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail="Email already registered"\n        )\n    \n    # Generate vault salt\n    vault_salt = VaultEncryption.generate_salt()\n    \n    # Create user\n    user = User(\n        email=user_data.email,\n        hashed_password=get_password_hash(user_data.password),\n        full_name=user_data.full_name,\n        master_password_hash=get_password_hash(user_data.master_password),\n        vault_salt=vault_salt.hex(),\n        is_verified=False  # Require email verification\n    )\n    \n    db.add(user)\n    await db.commit()\n    await db.refresh(user)\n    \n    # TODO: Send verification email\n    \n    return user\n\n\n@router.post("/login", response_model=Token)\nasync def login(\n    user_data: UserLogin,\n    request: Request,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Login user."""\n    \n    # Get user\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == user_data.email))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not user or not verify_password(user_data.password, user.hashed_password):\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Incorrect email or password"\n        )\n    \n    # Check if account is locked\n    if user.locked_until and user.locked_until > datetime.utcnow():\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="Account is temporarily locked. Please try again later."\n        )\n    \n    # Check if account is active\n    if not user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="Account is inactive"\n        )\n    \n    # Verify 2FA if enabled\n    if user.totp_enabled:\n        if not user_data.totp_code:\n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n                detail="2FA code required"\n            )\n        \n        if not verify_totp(user.totp_secret, user_data.totp_code):\n            # Increment failed attempts\n            user.failed_login_attempts += 1\n            \n            # Lock account after 5 failed attempts\n            if user.failed_login_attempts >= 5:\n                user.locked_until = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=30)\n            \n            await db.commit()\n            \n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n                detail="Invalid 2FA code"\n            )\n    \n    # Reset failed attempts\n    user.failed_login_attempts = 0\n    user.locked_until = None\n    user.last_login_at = datetime.utcnow()\n    user.last_login_ip = request.client.host if request.client else None\n    \n    # Create tokens\n    access_token = create_access_token({"sub": str(user.id)})\n    refresh_token = create_refresh_token({"sub": str(user.id)})\n    \n    # Create session\n    session = UserSession(\n        user_id=user.id,\n        refresh_token=refresh_token,\n        ip_address=request.client.host if request.client else None,\n        user_agent=request.headers.get("user-agent"),\n        expires_at=datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)\n    )\n    db.add(session)\n    \n    await db.commit()\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": access_token,\n        "refresh_token": refresh_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "expires_in": settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/refresh", response_model=Token)\nasync def refresh_token(\n    refresh_token: str,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Refresh access token."""\n    \n    # Decode refresh token\n    payload = decode_token(refresh_token)\n    if not payload or payload.get("type") != "refresh":\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid refresh token"\n        )\n    \n    # Get session\n    result = await db.execute(\n        select(UserSession).where(\n            UserSession.refresh_token == refresh_token,\n            UserSession.is_active == True\n        )\n    )\n    session = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not session or session.expires_at < datetime.utcnow():\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Invalid or expired refresh token"\n        )\n    \n    # Get user\n    result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.id == session.user_id))\n    user = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if not user or not user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="User not found or inactive"\n        )\n    \n    # Create new tokens\n    new_access_token = create_access_token({"sub": str(user.id)})\n    new_refresh_token = create_refresh_token({"sub": str(user.id)})\n    \n    # Update session\n    session.refresh_token = new_refresh_token\n    session.last_used_at = datetime.utcnow()\n    session.expires_at = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)\n    \n    await db.commit()\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": new_access_token,\n        "refresh_token": new_refresh_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "expires_in": settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/logout")\nasync def logout(\n    refresh_token: str,\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Logout user."""\n    \n    # Deactivate session\n    result = await db.execute(\n        select(UserSession).where(UserSession.refresh_token == refresh_token)\n    )\n    session = result.scalar_one_or_none()\n    \n    if session:\n        session.is_active = False\n        await db.commit()\n    \n    return {"message": "Logged out successfully"}\n\n\n@router.post("/2fa/setup", response_model=TOTPSetup)\nasync def setup_2fa(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Setup 2FA for user."""\n    \n    # Generate TOTP secret\n    secret = generate_totp_secret()\n    \n    # Save to user (but don\'t enable yet)\n    current_user.totp_secret = secret\n    await db.commit()\n    \n    # Generate QR code URI\n    qr_uri = get_totp_uri(secret, current_user.email)\n    \n    return {\n        "secret": secret,\n        "qr_code_uri": qr_uri\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/2fa/verify")\nasync def verify_2fa(\n    data: TOTPVerify,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Verify and enable 2FA."""\n    \n    if not current_user.totp_secret:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail="2FA not set up"\n        )\n    \n    # Verify code\n    if not verify_totp(current_user.totp_secret, data.code):\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail="Invalid 2FA code"\n        )\n    \n    # Enable 2FA\n    current_user.totp_enabled = True\n    \n    # Generate backup codes\n    backup_codes = [secrets.token_hex(4) for _ in range(10)]\n    current_user.backup_codes = ",".join(backup_codes)\n    \n    await db.commit()\n    \n    return {\n        "message": "2FA enabled successfully",\n        "backup_codes": backup_codes\n    }\n\n\n@router.post("/2fa/disable")\nasync def disable_2fa(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),\n    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)\n) -> Any:\n    """Disable 2FA."""\n    \n    current_user.totp_enabled = False\n    current_user.totp_secret = None\n    current_user.backup_codes = None\n    \n    await db.commit()\n    \n    return {"message": "2FA disabled successfully"}\n\n\n# Import get_current_user\nfrom ...api.deps import get_current_user\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

DATABASE_URL=postgresql://...\nrailway variables set REDIS_URL=redis://...\nrailway variables set SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key\nrailway variables set JWT_SECRET_KEY=your-jwt-secret\nrailway variables set MASTER_KEY=your-master-key\nrailway variables set VAULT_ENCRYPTION_KEY=your-vault-key\n```\n\n#### Database Setup on Railway\n```bash\n# Add PostgreSQL\nrailway add postgresql\n\n# Add Redis\nrailway add redis\n\n# Get connection strings\nrailway variables\n```\n\n### Option 2: Vercel (Recommended for Frontend)\n\n```bash\n# Install Vercel CLI\nnpm install -g vercel\n\n# Navigate to frontend\ncd passport/frontend\n\n# Deploy\nvercel\n\n# Set environment variables\nvercel env add NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL production\n# Enter: https://your-backend-url.railway.app\n\n# Deploy to Environment Configuration\n\n### Backend (.env)\n```bash\n# Application\nAPP_NAME=iTechSmart PassPort\nAPP_VERSION=1.0.0\nENVIRONMENT=production\nDEBUG=false\nSECRET_KEY=CHANGE_THIS_TO_RANDOM_32_CHAR_STRING\nAPI_V1_PREFIX=/api/v1\n\n# Server\nHOST=0.0.0.0\nPORT=8000\nWORKERS=4\n\n# Database\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://user:pass@host:5432/dbname\nDATABASE_POOL_SIZE=20\nDATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW=10\n\n# Redis\nREDIS_URL=redis://host:6379/0\nREDIS_PASSWORD=\nREDIS_DB=0\n\n# JWT\nJWT_SECRET_KEY=CHANGE_THIS_TO_RANDOM_32_CHAR_STRING\nJWT_ALGORITHM=HS256\nACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES=30\nREFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS=7\n\n# Encryption\nMASTER_KEY=CHANGE_THIS_TO_RANDOM_32_BYTE_STRING\nVAULT_ENCRYPTION_KEY=CHANGE_THIS_TO_RANDOM_32_BYTE_STRING\n\n# CORS\nCORS_ORIGINS=https://yourdomain.com,https://www.yourdomain.com\nCORS_ALLOW_CREDENTIALS=true\n\n# Rate Limiting\nRATE_LIMIT_PER_MINUTE=60\nRATE_LIMIT_PER_HOUR=1000\n\n# Email (SendGrid)\nSENDGRID_API_KEY=your_sendgrid_api_key\nFROM_EMAIL=noreply@yourdomain.com\nFROM_NAME=iTechSmart PassPort\n\n# Stripe\nSTRIPE_SECRET_KEY=sk_live_your_stripe_secret_key\nSTRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_live_your_stripe_publishable_key\nSTRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET=whsec_your_webhook_secret\nSTRIPE_PRICE_ID=price_your_price_id\n\n# Breach Monitoring\nHIBP_API_KEY=your_haveibeenpwned_api_key\n\n# AI Services (Optional)\nOPENAI_API_KEY=your_openai_api_key\nANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_anthropic_api_key\n\n# Monitoring\nSENTRY_DSN=your_sentry_dsn\nPROMETHEUS_PORT=9090\n\n# Logging\nLOG_LEVEL=INFO\nLOG_FORMAT=json\n```\n\n### Frontend (.env.local)\n```bash\nNEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://api.yourdomain.com\nNEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_live_your_stripe_key\n```\n\n### Generate Secure Keys\n```bash\n# Generate SECRET_KEY\npython -c "import secrets; Database Setup\n\n### Create Database\n```sql\n-- Connect to PostgreSQL\npsql -U postgres\n\n-- Create database\nCREATE DATABASE passport;\n\n-- Create user\nCREATE USER passport_user WITH PASSWORD \'secure_password\';\n\n-- Grant privileges\nGRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON DATABASE passport TO passport_user;\n\n-- Exit\n\\q\n```\n\n### Run Migrations\n```bash\ncd passport/backend\n\n# Initialize Alembic (if not done)\nalembic init alembic\n\n# Create migration\nalembic revision --autogenerate -m "Initial migration"\n\n# Apply migration\nalembic upgrade head\n\n# Rollback (if needed)\nalembic downgrade -1\n```\n\n### Create Admin User\n```python\n# create_admin.py\nimport asyncio\nfrom app.db.database import AsyncSessionLocal\nfrom app.models.user import User, UserRole\nfrom app.core.security import get_password_hash, VaultEncryption\n\nasync def create_admin():\n    async with AsyncSessionLocal() as db:\n        # Check if admin exists\n        from sqlalchemy import select\n        result = await db.execute(select(User).where(User.email == "admin@example.com"))\n        if result.scalar_one_or_none():\n            print("Admin user already exists")\n            return\n        \n        # Generate vault salt\n        vault_salt = VaultEncryption.generate_salt()\n        \n        # Create admin user\n        admin = User(\n            email="admin@example.com",\n            hashed_password=get_password_hash("Admin123!"),\n            full_name="Admin User",\n            master_password_hash=get_password_hash("AdminMaster123!"),\n            vault_salt=vault_salt.hex(),\n            role=UserRole.ADMIN,\n            is_verified=True,\n            is_active=True\n        )\n        \n        db.add(admin)\n        await db.commit()\n        print("Admin user created successfully")\n        print("Email: admin@example.com")\n        print("Password: Admin123!")\n        print("Master Password: AdminMaster123!")\n\nif __name__ == "__main__":\n    asyncio.run(create_admin())\n```\n\nRun:\n```bash\npython create_admin.py\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Security Checklist\n\n### Before Production\n- [ ] Change all default passwords\n- [ ] Generate secure random keys\n- [ ] Enable HTTPS/SSL\n- [ ] Configure CORS properly\n- [ ] Enable rate limiting\n- [ ] Setup firewall rules\n- [ ] Enable database backups\n- [ ] Setup monitoring\n- [ ] Configure logging\n- [ ] Review security headers\n- [ ] Enable 2FA for admin accounts\n- [ ] Setup Stripe webhooks\n- [ ] Configure email service\n- [ ] Test breach detection\n- [ ] Review API permissions\n- [ ] Setup error tracking (Sentry)\n\n### Security Headers (Nginx)\n```nginx\nadd_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;\nadd_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;\nadd_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;\nadd_header Referrer-Policy "no-referrer-when-downgrade" always;\nadd_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src \'self\' http: https: data: blob: \'unsafe-inline\'" always;\nadd_header Strict-Transport-Security "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains" always;\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8.
